Sub SetSpecValue(specName,
specValue)
	
Select
Case specName

Case
"#FIT"

gFit
specValue

Case
"#LEASE_TERM"
gLeaseTerm = specValue
Case "#SALES_DISCOUNT"

gSalesDiscount
specValue

Case
"#HIDE_MAT_COST_ON_BRIEFREPORT"
gBriefHideMaterialCost = specValue
Case "_NM_PREVIEW"

gPreviewOnScreen
(specValue > 0)
Select
	
'MsgBox specName
specValue
End Sub

Sub SetSpecValue(specName,
specValue)
	
Select
Case specName

Case
"_NM_JL_CUSTOMER_NAME"

gJobLocCompanyName
specValue

Case
"_NM_JL_BILLING_ADDRESS"

gJobLocAddress
=specValue
Case "_NM_JL_CITY"

gJobLocCity = specValue
Case "_NM_JL_STATE"
gJobLocState = specValue
Case "_NM_JL_ZIPCODE"
gJobLocZipCode = specValue
Case "_NM_JL_PHONE"
gJobLocPhone = specValue
Case "_NM_PREPRINTED"
gbPrintOnWhitePages
specValue

Case
"_NM_DOWNPAYMENT"
gDownPayment = specValue
Case "_NM_TERMSOFPAYMENT"
gTermsOfPayment
specValue

Case
"_NM_CONTRACTNUMBER"

gContractNumber = specValue
Case "_NM_PREVIEW"

gPreviewOnScreen
(specValue > 0)
' Added due by
SPR#247

Case
"#LEASE_TERM"
gMonthRental = specValue
Case "#FIT"
gFit = specValue
Case Else
'MsgBox
"SPEC
 " & specName
specValue
Select
	
'MsgBox "SPEC : 
specName & " = " & specValue
	End

change
	
'Write
Down Paiment
	
objXL.Worksheets("Agreement").Range("N32").Value
gDownPayment
	
'objXL.Worksheets("Agreement").Range("X29").Value = gTermsOfPayment
'Write a contract
number
	
objXL.Worksheets("Agreement").Range("G43").Value
gContractNumber
	
'Write
totals
Changed
by SPR#247
	
gTotalAmountOfContract
gMonthRate * gMonthRental
objXL.Worksheets("Agreement").Range("AD41").Value
gTotalAmountOfContract
	
objXL.Worksheets("Agreement").Range("AD42").Value = 0.0
' SDales
should be
zero For all Rental
Agreements,
SPR#247
!!!!
	
objXL.Worksheets("Agreement").Range("AD43").Value = gTotalAmountOfContract
'End
of Change
WriteRentalAgreementTerms()
End Sub
	'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	Sub
WriteRenewalRentalAgreement()
WriteRentalAgreementHeader()
	
objXL.Worksheets("RA2").Range("A1:AJ28").Copy(
objXL.Worksheets("Agreement").Range("A17") )
	
'Write
description
of all sections
objXL.Worksheets("Agreement").Range("A18").Value = gAllSectionsDescription
	
'Write
leasing
period
	
objXL.Worksheets("Agreement").Range("A31").Value
gMonthRental
	
'Write
maintenance
month
amount
	
'objXL.Worksheets("Agreement").Range("N31").Value = gMaitenancePerMonth
Changed
by SPR#247

'Write Month Rate
If (gMonthRental <>
0.0) Then

gMonthPrinciple = (gTotalParSel * (1
gMiscOverHead/100)/(1-gSalesCommission/100))/
gMonthRental
	
End If
If (gFit <>
0.0) Then

gMonthFIT = (gTotalParSel * (1
gMiscOverHead/100)/(1-gSalesCommission/100))*
gFit
	
End If
gMonthRate = Round(gMaitenancePerMonth + gMonthPrinciple + gMonthFIT,
	
objXL.Worksheets("Agreement").Range("N31").Value
gMonthRate
	'End of
change
	
'Write
Down Paiment
	
objXL.Worksheets("Agreement").Range("N32").Value
gDownPayment
'Write Macro
	
objXL.Worksheets("Agreement").Range("A37").Value
gMACRO99903
	
'Write
contract number
objXL.Worksheets("Agreement").Range("G43").Value = gContractNumber
'Write totals
' Changed due by
SPR#247
gTotalAmountOfContract = gMonthRate
gMonthRental
	
objXL.Worksheets("Agreement").Range("AD41").Value = gTotalAmountOfContract
objXL.Worksheets("Agreement").Range("AD42").Value
SDales tax should
be zero
Rental Agreements, SPR#247 !!!!
objXL.Worksheets("Agreement").Range("AD43").Value
gTotalAmountOfContract
	'End of
Change
	
WriteRentalAgreementTerms()
End Sub

	Sub
WriteSubsequentRenewalRentalAgreement()
WriteRentalAgreementHeader()
objXL.Worksheets("RA3").Range("A1:AJ28").Copy( objXL.Worksheets("Agreement").Range("A17")
'Write description of
sections
	
objXL.Worksheets("Agreement").Range("A18").Value
gAllSectionsDescription

period
	
objXL.Worksheets("Agreement").Range("A31").Value
gMonthRental
'Write maintenance per month amount
'objXL.Worksheets("Agreement").Range("N31").Value
gMaitenancePerMonth

SPR#247

Rate
	
If
(gMonthRental
<> 0.0)
Then
gMonthPrinciple
(gTotalParSel
(1 + gMiscOverHead/100)/(1-gSalesCommission/100))/ gMonthRental
	
If
(gFit
<> 0.0)
Then
gMonthFIT
(gTotalParSel
(1 + gMiscOverHead/100)/(1-gSalesCommission/100))* gFit
	
gMonthRate
Round(gMaitenancePerMonth
gMonthPrinciple
gMonthFIT, 2)

'End
of change

Function CalcBolt(mFilePath,mCentroid,mArea,mWind, mPipeDiam,mBoltCount,mBoltSpacing,mBoltDiam)
 Dim xlsbook
 Set xlsbook = CreateObject("Excel.Application")
 xlsbook.Visible = False
 xlsbook.Workbooks.Open
(mFilePath+"BoltBase.xls")
xlsbook.Workbooks("BoltBase.xls").Activate
xlsbook.Workbooks("BoltBase.xls").Worksheets("Bolt").Activate
 xlsbook.Workbooks("BoltBase.xls").Worksheets("Bolt").Range("A4").Value
mArea
 xlsbook.Workbooks("BoltBase.xls").Worksheets("Bolt").Range("B4").Value
mWind
 xlsbook.Workbooks("BoltBase.xls").Worksheets("Bolt").Range("J4").Value
mPipeDiam
 xlsbook.Workbooks("BoltBase.xls").Worksheets("Bolt").Range("F4").Value
mCentroid
 xlsbook.Workbooks("BoltBase.xls").Worksheets("Bolt").Range("B8").Value
mBoltCount
xlsbook.Workbooks("BoltBase.xls").Worksheets("Bolt").Range("A8").Value = mBoltSpacing
check
if desired bolt
diameter is
acceptable:

xlsbook.Workbooks("BoltBase.xls").Worksheets("Bolt").Calculate
	
sqarea
xlsbook.Workbooks("BoltBase.xls").Worksheets("Bolt").Cells(8,4).Value
 result
 For Each
Cell In
xlsbook.Workbooks("BoltBase.xls").Worksheets("Bolt").Range("B19:B32")
Cell.Value >sqarea Then
result = 0 Then
 result
Cell.Row
Next
	
minDiam = 0
If result
<> 0 Then

minDiam = xlsbook.Workbooks("BoltBase.xls").Worksheets("Bolt").Cells(result,
1).Value
	
else

CalcBolt

xlsbook.Workbooks("BoltBase.xls").Saved = TRUE

xlsbook.Application.Quit

Exit
function
	
end if
if minDiam > mBoltDiam then
xlsbook.Workbooks("BoltBase.xls").Worksheets("Bolt").Range("D11").Value
minDiam
else
 xlsbook.Workbooks("BoltBase.xls").Worksheets("Bolt").Range("D11").Value = mBoltDiam
	
end if

' now tell
to calculate
xlsbook.Workbooks("BoltBase.xls").Worksheets("Bolt").Calculate
lets gather
results
BoltDiam = 
xlsbook.Workbooks("BoltBase.xls").Worksheets("Bolt").Cells(11, 4).Value
VertEmbed
 xlsbook.Workbooks("BoltBase.xls").Worksheets("Bolt").Cells(10,
11).Value
InsideBendRadius = xlsbook.Workbooks("BoltBase.xls").Worksheets("Bolt").Cells(11,
11).Value
BendHorizLnth
xlsbook.Workbooks("BoltBase.xls").Worksheets("Bolt").Cells(12, 11).Value
	
ThreadLnth
xlsbook.Workbooks("BoltBase.xls").Worksheets("Bolt").Cells(13, 11).Value
	
TotalLnth = xlsbook.Workbooks("BoltBase.xls").Worksheets("Bolt").Cells(14,
11).Value
BaseMinLnth
xlsbook.Workbooks("BoltBase.xls").Worksheets("Bolt").Cells(7,
7).Value
	
BaseMinThick
xlsbook.Workbooks("BoltBase.xls").Worksheets("Bolt").Cells(7,
8).Value

xlsbook.Visible = True
xlsbook.Workbooks("BoltBase.xls").Saved
TRUE
	
'xlsbook.Workbooks("BoltBase.xls").Close
xlsbook.Application.Quit
	
'FindGusset (mFilePath, mPipeDiam)
'CalcBolt
'added
by WO7 item#2
CalcBolt = FindGusset
(mFilePath,
mPipeDiam)
	End
Function
	'Finds apropriate
Gusset
	Function FindGusset(mFilePath, mPipeDiam)
'mGussetThickness, mGussetLegLength) 
xlsbook1
xlsbook1 = CreateObject("Excel.Application")
xlsbook1.Workbooks.Open
(mFilePath+"Gusset.xls")
xlsbook1.Visible = False
xlsbook1.Workbooks("Gusset.xls").Activate
 result
 For Each
Cell In
xlsbook1.Workbooks("Gusset.xls").Worksheets("Gusset").Range("A19:A39")
Cell.Value =>
mPipeDiam
Then
If result
Then
result = Cell.Row
 End If
 End If
 Next
If result
<> 0 Then

GussetLegLength = xlsbook1.Workbooks("Gusset.xls").Worksheets("Gusset").Cells(result, 5).Value

GussetThickness = xlsbook1.Workbooks("Gusset.xls").Worksheets("Gusset").Cells(result, 6).Value
Else
FindGusset = 0

xlsbook1.Workbooks("Gusset.xls").Saved = TRUE

xlsbook1.Application.Quit
Exit function
 xlsbook1.Workbooks("Gusset.xls").Saved
TRUE
	
xlsbook1.Application.Quit
	
FindGusset
End Function
'----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
return values
BoltDiam
	VertEmbed
	InsideBendRadius = -1
BendHorizLnth = -1
ThreadLnth
	TotalLnth
	BaseMinLnth
	BaseMinThick = -1
GussetLegLength = -1
GussetThickness = -1

Function CalcSpread(mFilePath,mCentroid,mArea,mWind, mSignWt,mColWt,mMinSoilP,mMaxSoilP,mPipeDiam,mBaseLnth,mBaseRatio)
 Dim xlsbook
 Set xlsbook = CreateObject("Excel.Application")
 xlsbook.Workbooks.Open
(mFilePath+"SprFound.xls")
 xlsbook.Visible = True
 xlsbook.Workbooks("SprFound.xls").Activate
 xlsbook.Workbooks("SprFound.xls").Worksheets("Spread").Activate
xlsbook.Workbooks("SprFound.xls").Worksheets("Spread").Range("A4").Value = mArea
xlsbook.Workbooks("SprFound.xls").Worksheets("Spread").Range("B4").Value = mWind
xlsbook.Workbooks("SprFound.xls").Worksheets("Spread").Range("N4").Value = mSignWt
xlsbook.Workbooks("SprFound.xls").Worksheets("Spread").Range("L4").Value = mColWt
 xlsbook.Workbooks("SprFound.xls").Worksheets("Spread").Range("D4").Value
mMinSoilP
 xlsbook.Workbooks("SprFound.xls").Worksheets("Spread").Range("D5").Value
mMaxSoilP
 xlsbook.Workbooks("SprFound.xls").Worksheets("Spread").Range("J4").Value
mPipeDiam
 xlsbook.Workbooks("SprFound.xls").Worksheets("Spread").Range("F4").Value
mCentroid
 xlsbook.Workbooks("SprFound.xls").Worksheets("Spread").Range("B7").Value
mBaseLnth
 xlsbook.Workbooks("SprFound.xls").Worksheets("Spread").Range("C7").Value
mBaseRatio
possibly other data
values
tell to
calculate
 xlsbook.Workbooks("SprFound.xls").Worksheets("Spread").Calculate
 ' now lets
gather the results
result = 0
Each Cell
In xlsbook.Workbooks("SprFound.xls").Worksheets("Spread").Range("A11:A50")
If Cell.Value
True Then
result = 0 Then
 result
Cell.Row
Next
If result
<> 0 Then
MsgBox ("For debug only:I
found
it!")

FootDepth 
xlsbook.Workbooks("SprFound.xls").Worksheets("Spread").Cells(result, 2).Value

ConcrYards
xlsbook.Workbooks("SprFound.xls").Worksheets("Spread").Cells(result, 3).Value

FootDiamW 
xlsbook.Workbooks("SprFound.xls").Worksheets("Spread").Cells(7,
1).Value
FootDiamL
 = xlsbook.Workbooks("SprFound.xls").Worksheets("Spread").Cells(7, 2).Value

RebarNo3
xlsbook.Workbooks("SprFound.xls").Worksheets("Spread").Cells(result, 6).Value

RebarNo4
xlsbook.Workbooks("SprFound.xls").Worksheets("Spread").Cells(result, 4).Value

RebarNo6
xlsbook.Workbooks("SprFound.xls").Worksheets("Spread").Cells(result, 5).Value
 Else
 MsgBox
("For
debug
only:
Sorry, no
solutions
found!")
 FootDepth 
ConcrYards = -1

FootDiamW 
FootDiamL
 = -1

RebarNo3
RebarNo4 
 = -1

RebarNo6

'xlsbook.Visible
True
	
xlsbook.Workbooks("SprFound.xls").Saved = TRUE
xlsbook.Application.Quit
	
if
result <>
then
CalcSpread = 1
	
else
CalcSpread = 0
	
end if
End Function
'----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
return values
FootDepth 
	ConcrYards = -1
FootDiamW 
	FootDiamL
 = -1
RebarNo3
	RebarNo4 
 = -1
RebarNo6

	Function Parse(empList,
delimiter)
InStr(empList, delimiter)
<> 0 Then
 retValue
Left(empList,
pos-1)
empList
Right(empList, Len(empList)
pos)
Parse
retValue
Else
Parse
	End

Function
PrintEmployees (filePath,
empList, count,
mSortOrder)
xlsbook
CreateObject("Excel.Application")
xlsbook.Visible
True
 xlsbook.application.Workbooks.Add filePath+"\salary.xlt"
xlsbook.application.Workbooks("salary1").Activate
xlsbook.application.Workbooks("salary1").Worksheets("SALARIESFILE").Activate
 xlsbook.StatusBar = "Please be
patient
formatting in
progress..."
 WITH
xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.ActiveSheet
	
.Range("B1").Value
mSortOrder
	
empID = ""
empName

empRate = 0
	
FOR i = 0 TO
count
empID
Parse(empList, chr(9))

empName = Parse(empList,
chr(9))
empRate
Parse(empList, chr(9))
.Range("A3:C3").Copy
.Range("A4").Insert
.Range("A4").Value = empID
.Range("B4").Value = empName
.Range("C4").Value = empRate

NEXT
.Range("A3:C3").EntireRow.Delete
.Range("A3:C3").EntireRow.Delete
IF (InStr
(1,mSortOrder,"ID")
or (InStr
(1,mSortOrder,"id")
THEN

.Range
("A3:C"&(3+count)).Sort
.Range ("A3")

ELSE
.Range ("A3:C"&(3+count)).Sort .Range
("B3")
	
END IF
 END WITH
 xlsbook.StatusBar = FALSE
save current sheet in
case user
won't
be asked various questions:
 xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.Saved
TRUE
xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.ActiveSheet.Range("A1").Activate
	End
Function

dim ColWidth
ColWidth
Array
(7 ,10,
	Function PrintReport
 Set xlsbook = CreateObject("Excel.Application")
 xlsbook.Visible = True
xlsbook.Workbooks.Add
CsvFileName
xlsbook.StatusBar
"Please
be patient - formatting
in progress..."
WITH xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.ActiveSheet
change font
text
.Cells.Font.Name = "Arial
Narrow"

FOR i = 1 to

.Columns(i).ColumnWidth = ColWidth(i-1) 

.Columns(i).Borders.LineStyle = 1
NEXT


.Columns(4).NumberFormat
"$#,##0.00"

' locate
last record
(every cell
in column
contains a value):
	
lastRow = .Columns(2).End(4).Row
TO lastRow
IF not IsNumeric(.Cells(i,1).Value)
or IsEmpty(.Cells(i,1).Value)
THEN

.Rows(i).Font.Bold= TRUE
.Rows(i).Font.Size=
	
NEXT

' setup page
headers: insert
report title & page
	
.PageSetup.CenterHeader = "&CMATERIAL LIST
REPORT"
.PageSetup.RightHeader = "&RDate of
Report:
.PageSetup.CenterFooter
"&CPage
&P of
.PageSetup.Orientation = 1
	
.PageSetup.CenterHorizontally = FALSE
.PageSetup.CenterVertically

.PageSetup.LeftMargin

.PageSetup.RightMargin = xlsbook.InchesToPoints(0.25)
 .PageSetup.TopMargin
xlsbook.InchesToPoints(0.77)
.PageSetup.BottomMargin
xlsbook.InchesToPoints(0.75)
.PageSetup.HeaderMargin
xlsbook.InchesToPoints(0.5)
 .PageSetup.FooterMargin = xlsbook.InchesToPoints(0.5)
.PageSetup.PrintHeadings = FALSE
.PageSetup.PrintGridlines
FALSE
 END WITH
 xlsbook.StatusBar = FALSE
save current sheet in
case user
won't
be asked various questions:
 xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.Saved
TRUE
End Function

Function
PrintReport
xlsbook
CreateObject("Excel.Application")
xlsbook.Visible
True
 xlsbook.Workbooks.Add CsvFileName
 xlsbook.StatusBar = "Please be
patient
formatting in
progress..."
 WITH
xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.ActiveSheet
.Columns(1).ColumnWidth
.Columns(2).ColumnWidth
.Columns(3).ColumnWidth
.Columns(4).ColumnWidth
.Columns(3).NumberFormat = "mm/dd/yyyy"

.Columns(4).NumberFormat
"$#,##0.00"
 ' paste headers
	
.rows(1).Insert
	
.Cells(1,1).Value = "Design #"
.Cells(1,1).WrapText = TRUE
.Cells(1,2).Value
"Customer"
	
.Cells(1,2).WrapText
TRUE
	
.Cells(1,3).Value = "Date"

.Cells(1,3).WrapText
TRUE
.Cells(1,4).Value
"Selling Price"

.Cells(1,4).WrapText
TRUE
underline
this:

.Rows(1).Borders(4).LineStyle = 1
.rows(1).Insert

.Cells(1,3).Value = "Ordered
by:"
.Cells(1,3).HorizontalAlignment
right

.Cells(1,4).Value = mOrderType

.Cells(1,4).HorizontalAlignment = 2 ' left

' underline it:
.Range("C1:D1").Borders(4).LineStyle = 1
totals:

lastRow = .Columns(3).End(4).Row

.cells(lastRow+1,3).Value = "Total
Estimated
Selling
Price:"

.Cells(lastRow+1,3).HorizontalAlignment = 4 ' right
.cells(lastRow+1,4).Value
"=Sum(D3:D"&(lastRow)&")"

.cells(lastRow+2,3).Value = "Total
Number of
Estimates:"

.Cells(lastRow+2,3).HorizontalAlignment = 4 ' right
.cells(lastRow+2,4).Value
"=Count(D3:D"&(lastRow)&")"
.Cells(lastRow+2,4).NumberFormat = "General"

underline
last row before
totals:
.Rows(lastRow).Borders(4).LineStyle
	
' sort
items
in given order:
searchText = UCase(mOrderType)
	
if
(InStr(1,searchText,"CUSTOMER")
then
.Range("A3:D"&lastRow).Sort
.Range("B2")
	
else

.Range("A3:D"&lastRow).Sort .Range("A2")
setup
page headers:
insert report
title
page #s
.PageSetup.CenterHeader
"OPEN
ESTIMATE REPORT"
	
.PageSetup.RightHeader
"&RDate
of Report: &D"
.PageSetup.CenterFooter
"&CPage
&P of

 xlsbook.StatusBar = FALSE
save current sheet in
case user
won't
be asked various questions:
 xlsbook.activeworkbook.Saved
TRUE
End Function

Function
Print_footer(copy_text)
xlsbook.activeworkbook.sheets(copy_text).PageSetup.LeftFooter
"&L"&mWONumber
	
xlsbook.activeworkbook.sheets(copy_text).PageSetup.RightFooter
"&R"&copy_text
	End

	'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	Function print_work_and_material_form
(copy_text,
startRow)
dim pasteRow
paste
work descr page
PasteHeader
 MatFrmPageRange,"Templates",copy_text,
startRow
	
' put design
	
pasteRow
startRow+2
	
PutValue
copy_text, "C"&pasteRow, mDesignNo
	
' put work
order
	
pasteRow
startRow
	
PutValue
copy_text, "Q"&pasteRow, mWONumber
	
' today's date:
	
PutValue
copy_text, "Q"&(pasteRow+1), CDate(now())
copy text
pasteRow = startRow+1
PutValue copy_text,
"A"&pasteRow,
copy_text
do nothing more.
	
print_footer
copy_text
End Function
'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Function
print_additional_description (copy_text, nSymbolsOnRight)
dim printText
	
' insert
additional page
description
PasteHeader
AdditPageRange,"Templates",copy_text,pageEndTopPage
name of
copy
	
PutValue
copy_text, "A"&(pageEndTopPage+1), copy_text
	
' design
	
PutValue
copy_text, "C"&(pageEndTopPage+2), mDesignNo
	
' today's date:
	
PutValue
copy_text, "Q"&(pageEndTopPage+1), CDate(now())
wo number
PutValue copy_text,
"Q"&pageEndTopPage,
mWONumber
	
printText = Right(mWorkDescr,nSymbolsOnRight)
	
PutValue
copy_text, "A"&(pageEndTopPage+6), printText
	
SetRowHt
copy_text, pageEndTopPage+6, 224
	
PutValue
copy_text, "M11",
"IVC_"&mWONumber
	
print_footer
copy_text
end Function

	Function print_shipping_installation (copy_text)
	dim
shipInstr
dim nCharsLeft
shipInstr
	
' depending on
shipping type:
	
if
(mShipType = "SHIPTO") then

shipInstr = "Ship This
Order
to Customer
"+mShipVia
	
end if
if (mShipType
"INSTALL") then

shipInstr = "Install
This Order"
	
if
(mShipType = "DROP") then

shipInstr = "Drop Ship
This Order via "+mShipVia
	
if
(mShipType = "PICKUP") then

shipInstr = "Customer Pick-up / No
Shipping Required
	
' if
length of
resulting
text exceeds maximum of
80 chars,
break
it into
pieces
	
nCharsLeft
Len(shipInstr)
	
if
(nCharsLeft
MAX_CHARS_IN_SHIPPING) then

PutValue
copy_text, "E41",Left(shipInstr,MAX_CHARS_IN_SHIPPING)
PutValue copy_text,
"A42",Right(shipInstr,nCharsLeft - MAX_CHARS_IN_SHIPPING)
else
PutValue copy_text,
"E41", shipInstr
	
end if
contact
person
	
PutValue
copy_text, "C43",
mContactPerson
	
' put company nanme
	
PutValue
copy_text, "C44",
mShipName
street address
	
PutValue
copy_text, "C45",
mShipAddress
	
' put city
PutValue copy_text,
"C46", mShipCity
	
' put state
	
PutValue
copy_text, "C47",
mShipState
	
' put zip
	
PutValue
copy_text, "G47",
mShipZipCode
	
' put phone no
PutValue copy_text,
"C48", mShipPhone
'put 
freight
charges
PutValue copy_text,
"M47", mPayType
install
street address
	
PutValue
copy_text, "L43",
mInstallAddress
install
city
	
PutValue
copy_text, "L44",
mInstallCity
	
' put install state
	
PutValue
copy_text, "L45",
mInstallState
install
PutValue copy_text,
"P45", mInstallZipCode
	End

Function
print_financial_section
(copy_text,
print_money)
	dim
discount_amnt
if (print_money
TRUE)
then
calc selling price line:
discount_amnt
mTotalEstCharges * (1
mSalesDiscount/100)-1)
gross
sale amount:
PutValue copy_text,
"C36", mTotalEstCharges+discount_amnt

' put discount
amount
PutValue copy_text,
"H36", discount_amnt
discount percent:

PutValue
copy_text, "M36",
mSalesDiscount/100
sale:

PutValue
copy_text, "P36",
mTotalEstCharges
'put total charges
PutValue copy_text,
"C37", mTotalInvoiceAmnt
deposite received

PutValue
copy_text, "I37",
mDepositAmnt
balance
due:
PutValue copy_text,
"P37", mRemainingBalance
	
end if
	End

permit_fee

"D33", mTax

calculated by
excel

' PutValue
copy_text, "D33",
mTotalInvoiceAmnt
else
print
nothing.
	
end if
	end

	Function Print_header_and_description

' wo
number

today's
date:

"Q2",
CDate(now())
	
' our company name
PutValue copy_text,
"E3",
OurCompanyName
	
' our company address
	
PutValue
copy_text, "A4", OurCompanyAddr
company
city
	
PutValue
copy_text, "A5", OurCompanyCity
customer info
cust name

"C6",
mBillName
billing
address

"I6",
mBillAddress
	
' city

"O6",
mBillCity
state
PutValue copy_text,
"B8",
mBillState
	
' zip code
PutValue copy_text,
"F8",
mBillZipCode
	
' phone
	
PutValue
copy_text, "I8", mBillPhone
PutValue copy_text,
"O8",
mBillFaxNo
	
' calc
amount of
chars
that may be
fitted to
first
page of
description:
	
SetRowHt
copy_text, 10, 112 ' height
of row

if (nTotalChars
MAX_CHARS_IN_FIRST_PAGE
then
only first 1000
chars
to first page

PutValue
copy_text, "A10",
Left(mWorkDescr,MAX_CHARS_IN_FIRST_PAGE

Print_header_and_description
nTotalChars
MAX_CHARS_IN_FIRST_PAGE
	
else

' put all text

copy_text, "A10",
mWorkDescr
Print_header_and_description = 0
	
end If
	
PutValue
copy_text, "M11",
"IVC_"&mWONumber
	End

	'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	Function Print_1_job_order(copy_text,
print_money)
	dim
nSymbolsLeftCount
time I am
called,must
create new sheet with
given
name and work
with it
xlsbook.activeworkbook.Sheets.Add
 xlsbook.activeworkbook.activesheet.name = copy_text
 ' put page
header
 xlsbook.activeworkbook.sheets(copy_text).PageSetup.RightHeader
"&RPage
&P of
page margins
 SetMargins
copy_text
 GatherColumnWidths
 "templates","A1:R1"
 PasteHeader StartPageRange
"Templates", copy_text,1
 RestoreColumnWidths copy_text,"A1:R1"
 nSymbolsLeftCount = print_header_and_description( copy_text)
print_some_office_info copy_text
print_charge_cost_section
copy_text, print_money
 print_financial_section 
 copy_text,
print_money
print_shipping_installation
copy_text
print_footer copy_text
 AddPageBreak
copy_text, pageEndTopPage
(nSymbolsLeftCount >0) then
print_additional_description copy_text,
nSymbolsLeftCount
AddPageBreak copy_text,
pageEndTopPage+AdditPageHt
	
print_1_job_order = pageEndTopPage+AdditPageHt
else
print_1_job_order
pageEndTopPage
 end if
End Function

Function
	'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	Function RestoreColumnWidths(sheet,
range)
	dim
to nColumnCount
 xlsbook.activeworkbook.sheets(sheet).Range(range).Columns(i).ColumnWidth
ClmnWidth
next 
End Function
'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Function
GatherColumnWidths(sheet,
range)
	dim
nColumnCount = xlsbook.activeworkbook.sheets(sheet).Range(range).Columns.Count
	
for i = 1 to
nColumnCount

with
xlsbook.activeworkbook.sheets(sheet).Range(range).Columns(i)
ClmnWidth(i) = .ColumnWidth
with
	
next
	End
Function
	'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	Function FitLine (copy_text,range)
	
xlsbook.activeworkbook.sheets(copy_text).Range(range).Rows.AutoFit
End Function
'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Function
Msg( text)
	
if
mydebug
"TRUE" then

msgbox(text)
	End
Function
	'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	Function UnderLine (range)
	 xlsbook.application.activeworkbook.activesheet.Range(range).Borders(4).LineStyle
End Function
'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Function
SetRowHt (copy_text,row, value)
xlsbook.activeworkbook.sheets(copy_text).Rows(row).RowHeight = value
	end
Function
	'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	Function SetMargins
copy_text)
	 dim pageObj
	 set pageObj = xlsbook.activeworkbook.sheets("templates").PageSetup
With xlsbook.activeworkbook.sheets(copy_text).PageSetup
 .PaperSize
pageObj.PaperSize
 .Orientation
pageObj.Orientation
 .PrintGridLines = pageObj.PrintGridLines
 .PrintHeadings
pageObj.PrintHeadings
 .PrintTitleColumns
pageObj.PrintTitleColumns
 .PrintTitleRows = pageObj.PrintTitleRows
 .LeftMargin = pageObj.LeftMargin
 .RightMargin
pageObj.RightMargin
 .TopMargin
pageObj.TopMargin
 .BottomMargin = pageObj.BottomMargin
 .HeaderMargin = pageObj.HeaderMargin
 .FooterMargin = pageObj.FooterMargin
 .Zoom

 = pageObj.Zoom
End With
End Function
'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Function
SetEnvelopMargins
copy_text)
	 dim pageObj
	 set pageObj = xlsbook.activeworkbook.sheets("Envelop
temp").PageSetup
	 With
xlsbook.activeworkbook.sheets(copy_text).PageSetup
.PaperSize = pageObj.PaperSize
.Orientation = pageObj.Orientation
.PrintGridLines
pageObj.PrintGridLines
.PrintHeadings = pageObj.PrintHeadings
.PrintTitleColumns = pageObj.PrintTitleColumns
.PrintTitleRows
pageObj.PrintTitleRows
.LeftMargin
pageObj.LeftMargin
.RightMargin = pageObj.RightMargin
.TopMargin = pageObj.TopMargin
.BottomMargin
pageObj.BottomMargin
.HeaderMargin
pageObj.HeaderMargin
.FooterMargin
pageObj.FooterMargin
.Zoom
pageObj.Zoom
	End
With
	End
Function
	'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	Function AddPageBreak
copy_text,rowIndex )
	 xlsbook.activeworkbook.sheets(copy_text).Rows(rowIndex).PageBreak = 1
	End

	'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	Function Pasteheader (from,
source,dest, pasteRow)
	
xlsbook.activeworkbook.sheets(source).Range(from).Copy
xlsBook.activeworkbook.sheets(dest).Range("A"&pasteRow).PasteSpecial
	End
Function
	'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	Function PutValue(dest,
range, value)
xlsbook.activeworkbook.sheets(dest).Range(range).Value 
value
End Function

Function
PrintReport
dim startRow
xlsbook
CreateObject("Excel.Application")
xlsbook.Workbooks.Add
filePath+"\job_order.xlt"
xlsbook.Visible
True
xlsbook.StatusBar
"Please
be patient - formatting
in progress..."
(mOfficeCopy = "TRUE") then

print_1_job_order "OFFICE COPY",
TRUE 
(mPrintSellPriceYesNo
"TRUE")
then
startRow = print_1_job_order ("SHOP
COPY", TRUE)
 else

startRow
print_1_job_order
("SHOP COPY",
FALSE)
 end if
print_work_and_material_form "SHOP COPY",
startRow
Create_envelop "Envelop",
FALSE
delete templates sheet:
xlsbook.DisplayAlerts
 = FALSE
 xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.Sheets("Templates").Delete 
 xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.Sheets("Envelop
temp").Delete
xlsbook.DisplayAlerts
TRUE
clean
clipboard
activate top of
report
WITH xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook
.ActiveSheet.Range("A1").copy
xlsbook.CutCopyMode
FALSE
.Saved = TRUE
.ActiveSheet.Range("A1").Activate
 END WITH
 xlsbook.StatusBar = FALSE
	End

discount amount

"P39", mTotalEstCharges
else
clear
line of
money

' add page

descr
page needed

then
print_additional_description copy_text,
nSymbolsLeftCount

' add page

	'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	Function print_shipping_installation (copy_text, startRow)
	
shipInstr = ""
depending
on shipping
type:
if (mShipType
"SHIPTO")
then
shipInstr
"Ship
This Order to
Customer via "+mShipVia
	
if
(mShipType = "INSTALL")
then
shipInstr
"Install This
Order"
	
end if
if (mShipType
"DROP")
then
shipInstr
"Drop
Ship This
Order
"+mShipVia
	
end if
if (mShipType
"PICKUP")
then
shipInstr
"Customer
Pick-up
No Shipping
Required "
	
end if
if length
of resulting text
exceeds
maximum
of 80
chars,
	
' break it
into two pieces
nCharsLeft = Len(shipInstr)
if (nCharsLeft > MAX_CHARS_IN_SHIPPING)
then
PutValue copy_text,
"E"&(startRow+1),Left(shipInstr,MAX_CHARS_IN_SHIPPING)
PutValue copy_text,
"A"&(startRow+2),Right(shipInstr,nCharsLeft
MAX_CHARS_IN_SHIPPING)
	
else

PutValue
copy_text, "E"&(startRow+1), shipInstr
	
end if
contact
person
	
PutValue
copy_text, "C"&(startRow+4), mContactPerson
company
nanme
PutValue copy_text,
"C"&(startRow+5),
mShipName
street address
	
PutValue
copy_text, "C"&(startRow+6), mShipAddress
city
	
PutValue
copy_text, "C"&(startRow+7), mShipCity
	
' put state
	
PutValue
copy_text, "C"&(startRow+8), mShipState
PutValue copy_text,
"G"&(startRow+8),
mShipZipCode
	
' put phone no
PutValue copy_text,
"C"&(startRow+9),
mShipPhone
	
'put
 freight charges
	
PutValue
copy_text, "M"&(startRow+8), mPayType
	
if
(copy_text = "SHOP COPY")
then
nothing
else
designer name:
PutValue copy_text,
"C"&(startRow+21), mArtist
design no:
PutValue copy_text,
"C"&(startRow+22), mDesignNo
	
end if
End Function

Function
print_financial_section
(copy_text)
calc selling price line:

gross
sale amount:

copy_text, "C38",
mTotalEstCharges+discount_amnt
	
' put discount
amount
	
PutValue
copy_text, "H38",
discount_amnt
discount percent:
PutValue copy_text,
"M38", mSalesDiscount/100
sale:
PutValue copy_text,
"P38", mTotalEstCharges
'put total charges
	
PutValue
copy_text, "C39",
mTotalInvoiceAmnt
deposite received
PutValue copy_text,
"I39", mDepositAmnt
balance
due:
	
PutValue
copy_text, "P39",
mRemainingBalance
End Function

(mWorkDescr)

text

	End

Function
	'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	Function RestoreColumnWidths(sheet,
range)
	
for i = 1 to
nColumnCount
xlsbook.activeworkbook.sheets(sheet).Range(range).Columns(i).ColumnWidth = ClmnWidth (i)
	
next
	End
Function
	'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	Function GatherColumnWidths(sheet, range)
nColumnCount = xlsbook.application.activeworkbook.sheets(sheet).Range(range).Columns.Count
	
for i = 1 to
nColumnCount

with
xlsbook.application.activeworkbook.sheets(sheet).Range(range).Columns(i)
ClmnWidth(i) = .ColumnWidth
with
	
next
	End
Function
	'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	Function FitLine (copy_text,range)
	
xlsbook.activeworkbook.sheets(copy_text).Range(range).Rows.AutoFit
End Function
'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Function
UnderLine
(range)
xlsbook.activeworkbook.sheets("").Range(range).Borders(4).LineStyle
End Function
'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Function
SetRowHt (copy_text,row, value)
xlsbook.activeworkbook.sheets(copy_text).Rows(row).RowHeight = value
	end
Function
	'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	Function SetMargins
copy_text)
	 dim pageObj
	 set pageObj = xlsbook.activeworkbook.sheets("templates").PageSetup
With xlsbook.activeworkbook.sheets(copy_text).PageSetup
 .PaperSize
pageObj.PaperSize
 .Orientation
pageObj.Orientation
 .PrintGridLines = pageObj.PrintGridLines
 .PrintHeadings
pageObj.PrintHeadings
 .PrintTitleColumns
pageObj.PrintTitleColumns
 .PrintTitleRows = pageObj.PrintTitleRows
 .LeftMargin = pageObj.LeftMargin
 .RightMargin
pageObj.RightMargin
 .TopMargin
pageObj.TopMargin
 .BottomMargin = pageObj.BottomMargin
 .HeaderMargin = pageObj.HeaderMargin
 .FooterMargin = pageObj.FooterMargin
 .Zoom

 = pageObj.Zoom
End With
End Function
'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Function
SetEnvelopMargins
copy_text)
	 dim pageObj
	 set pageObj = xlsbook.activeworkbook.sheets("Envelop
temp").PageSetup
	 With
xlsbook.activeworkbook.sheets(copy_text).PageSetup
.PaperSize = pageObj.PaperSize
.Orientation = pageObj.Orientation
.PrintGridLines
pageObj.PrintGridLines
.PrintHeadings = pageObj.PrintHeadings
.PrintTitleColumns = pageObj.PrintTitleColumns
.PrintTitleRows
pageObj.PrintTitleRows
.LeftMargin
pageObj.LeftMargin
.RightMargin = pageObj.RightMargin
.TopMargin = pageObj.TopMargin
.BottomMargin
pageObj.BottomMargin
.HeaderMargin
pageObj.HeaderMargin
.FooterMargin
pageObj.FooterMargin
.Zoom
pageObj.Zoom
	End
With
	End

copy_text,rowIndex )
	 xlsbook.activeworkbook.sheets(copy_text).Rows(rowIndex).PageBreak = 1
	End

	'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	Function Pasteheader (from,
source,
dest,
pasteRow)
xlsbook.activeworkbook.sheets(source).Range(from).Copy
	
xlsBook.activeworkbook.sheets(dest).Range("A"&pasteRow).PasteSpecial
page header
if (source = "Templates")
then
xlsbook.activeworkbook.sheets(dest).PageSetup.RightHeader
"&RPage
&P of
	End

	'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	Function PutValue(dest,

xlsbook.activeworkbook.sheets(dest).Range(range).Value 
value
End Function

(copy_text,

End Function

Function
PrintReport
xlsbook
CreateObject("Excel.Application")
xlsbook.Workbooks.Add
filePath+"\manuf_order.xlt"
xlsbook.Visible
True
xlsbook.StatusBar
"Please
be patient - formatting
in progress..."
 ' office
shop copies
printed
always together, so:
 ' print office
copy
 print_office_copy "OFFICE COPY"
 ' save
current
sheet
in case
user won't be
asked
various
questions:
 xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.Saved
TRUE
 ' print shop
copy
 startRow
print_shop_copy
("SHOP COPY")
if additional
pages
required,
print
them:
if (mPrintInstPage = "TRUE") then

startRow
printInstPage
("SHOP COPY",startRow)
AddPageBreak "SHOP COPY",
startRow
 end if
if (mPrintQAPage = "TRUE") then

startRow
printQAPage("SHOP
COPY",startRow)

AddPageBreak
"SHOP
COPY", startRow
(mPrintLaborPage = "TRUE") then

startRow
printLaborPage ("SHOP
COPY", startRow)
AddPageBreak "SHOP COPY",
startRow
 end if
 Create_envelop
"Envelop", FALSE
 ' delete
templates
sheet:
 xlsbook.DisplayAlerts 
FALSE
xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.Sheets("Templates").Delete
xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.Sheets("Envelop temp").Delete
 xlsbook.DisplayAlerts = TRUE
 ' clean clipboard and activate
of report
 WITH
xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook

.ActiveSheet.Range("A1").copy

xlsbook.CutCopyMode = FALSE

.Saved
TRUE

.ActiveSheet.Range("A1").Activate
WITH
xlsbook.StatusBar
FALSE
End Function

'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
' note
difference from
other
similar
in other scripts:
this fn
pastes to
region of
' the same
shape
as selection.
Function
PasteLine
(from, pasteRow)
	
xlsbook.application.activeworkbook.activesheet.Rows(pasteRow).Insert
xlsbook.application.activeworkbook.activesheet.Range(from).Copy
xlsBook.Application.activeworkbook.activesheet.Range("A"&pasteRow&":I"&pasteRow).PasteSpecial
End Function
'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Function
PutValue(range,
value)
	
xlsbook.application.activeworkbook.activesheet.Range(range).Value 
value
End Function
'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Function
Parse(text,
delimiter)
InStr(text,
delimiter)
If pos <>
Then
retValue = Left(text,
pos-1)
text = Right(text, Len(text) - pos)
 Parse = retValue
 Else
 Parse = ""
 End If
End Function
'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Function
PrintReport
xlsbook
CreateObject("Excel.Application")
xlsbook.application.Workbooks.Add
filePath+"\sales_perform.xlt"
xlsbook.application.Workbooks("sales_perform1").Activate
 xlsbook.application.Workbooks("sales_perform1").Sheets("SalesMenPerformance").Activate
xlsbook.application.Visible
True
 xlsbook.StatusBar = "Please be
patient
formatting in
progress..." 
start
year/month:
yearValue
 DatePart("yyyy",mStartDate)
 monthValue
DatePart ("m", mStartDate)
 PutValue
"B1",
monthValue & "/" & yearValue
'put end year/month
yearValue
 DatePart("yyyy",mEndDate)
 monthValue
DatePart ("m", mEndDate)
(monthValue
1) then

yearValue = yearValue -1

monthValue
 else

monthValue
monthValue -1
PutValue "D1", monthValue
yearValue
 ' now parse the statistics
itself:
nDeptCount = Parse (rText,chr(9))
pasteRow = 4
 for i=1 to
nDeptCount 

'paste
newline:
PasteLine
"A3:I3",pasteRow

' get sales person
name

descr = Parse(rText,chr(9))

PutValue
"A"&pasteRow,
descr

' get estimates bid

descr = Parse(rText,chr(9))

PutValue
"B"&pasteRow,
descr
estimates
descr
Parse(rText,chr(9))
PutValue "C"&pasteRow, descr
	
' get amount
descr
Parse(rText,chr(9))
PutValue "E"&pasteRow, descr
pasteRow = pasteRow
next
 ' now remove
empty
line:
xlsbook.application.activeworkbook.activesheet.Rows(3).Delete
clean
clipboard
activate top of
report
WITH xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook
.ActiveSheet.Range("A1").copy
xlsbook.CutCopyMode
FALSE
.Saved = TRUE
.ActiveSheet.Range("A1").Activate
 END WITH
 xlsbook.StatusBar = FALSE
	End
Function	
xlsbook

'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Function
PutValue(range,
value)
	
xlsbook.application.activeworkbook.activesheet.Range(range).Value

'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Then
retValue = Left(text,

 Parse = retValue
 Else

End Function

pasteRow = 4
 for i=1 to
nDeptCount 

'paste
newline:
PasteLine
"A3:I3",pasteRow

' get department

descr = Parse(rText,chr(9))

PutValue
"A"&pasteRow,
descr

' get dept
name

descr = Parse(rText,chr(9))

PutValue
"B"&pasteRow,
descr
estmat

descr = Parse(rText,chr(9))

PutValue
"C"&pasteRow,
descr
actmat 
descr
Parse(rText,chr(9))
PutValue "D"&pasteRow, descr
	
' get estLab
descr
Parse(rText,chr(9))
PutValue "G"&pasteRow, descr
	
' get actLab
descr
Parse(rText,chr(9))
PutValue "H"&pasteRow, descr
pasteRow = pasteRow
next
 ' now update
line of
totals:
PutValue "C"&pasteRow, "=Sum(C2:C"&(pasteRow-1)&")"
PutValue "D"&pasteRow, "=Sum(D2:D"&(pasteRow-1)&")"
PutValue "G"&pasteRow, "=Sum(G2:G"&(pasteRow-1)&")"
PutValue "H"&pasteRow, "=Sum(H2:H"&(pasteRow-1)&")"
remove empty line:
 xlsbook.activeworkbook.activesheet.Rows(3).Delete
 ' clean clipboard and activate
of report
 WITH
xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook

.ActiveSheet.Range("A1").copy

xlsbook.CutCopyMode = FALSE

.Saved
TRUE

.ActiveSheet.Range("A1").Activate
WITH
xlsbook.StatusBar
FALSE
End Function

	'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	Function UpdateOrderSheetDates (sheetName, fileName)
	
xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.sheets(sheetName).Activate
	
' 1)
locate first free
writing:
	
freeRow = FindFreeRowAny
(sheetName,"A6:A506")
IF freeRow = -1
THEN
freeRow
	
' 2)
thru range of
existing values
testing
if given wo
number is
written
already:
	
existingRow = FindValueRow
(sheetName,"A6:A"&freeRow,mWONumber, "A6")
	
IF
existingRow
-1 THEN

' sorry,
requested
order
found. Warn
User about error.

ErrorText = "Order
Entry
Journal: "&fileName&CHR(13)& _
"Sheet "&sheetName&CHR(13)&
 "Sorry, but requested "&sheetName&" order with
number "&mWONumber&" was not found!"
ErrorText
ErrorText
chr(10)+"Can not update
work order date
of completion."

CloseExcel

Err.Raise 1,,ErrorText
ELSE
IF mHandleCloseDate
"CLOSE"
THEN

' create
date of
completion;
storeValue = now
ELSE

storeValue

END IF
(sheetName = "SHOP") THEN
PutValue sheetName,
"H"&existingRow, storeValue

ELSE
PutValue sheetName,
"I"&existingRow, storeValue

END IF
	End

	'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	Function UpdateOrderSheet
(sheetName,
fileName)
xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.sheets(sheetName).Activate
1) locate
first
free row for writing:

freeRow = FindFreeRowAny
(sheetName,"A6:A506")
IF freeRow = -1
THEN
oops,
no free
rows for pasting.Warn
User.

CloseExcel

Err.Raise 1,,"Order Entry Journal:"&fileName&CHR(13)& _
"Sheet "&sheetName&CHR(13)&
 " Sorry,
we can not paste more
than 500 records per sheet in
month."
	
' 2)
thru range of
existing values
testing
if given wo
number is
written
already:
	
existingRow = FindValueRow
(sheetName,"A6:A"&freeRow,mWONumber, "A6")
	
IF
existingRow
-1 THEN

' ok, can safely
paste
data

(sheetName = "SHOP") THEN
PasteOrderShopDataLine sheetName,
freeRow

ELSE
PasteOrderDataLine sheetName,freeRow
	
ELSE

' oops, journal already contains
this work
order.
user if
he wants to
overwrite
record.

SelectLine
sheetName, existingRow
retValue = MsgBox
("Order
Entry
Journal
"&fileName&chr(13)&

"Sheet
"&sheetName&chr(13)& _
"Work
Order
with number
"&mWONumber&"
exists already!"&

chr(13)&"Do you wish
to replace it?",4,"Error")
IF retValue
THEN ' 6 = yes

' now can replace it
IF (sheetName
"SHOP")
THEN
PasteOrderShopDataLine sheetName,
existingRow
ELSE
PasteOrderDataLine sheetName,existingRow

END IF

ELSE
CloseExcel

Err.Raise 1,,"Order Entry Journal "&fileName&CHR(13)& _
 "Sheet
"&sheetName&CHR(13)& _
 "Work Order "&mWONumber&" record
insert canceled
at the user
request."

END IF
	end

	'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	Function UpdateProdSheet (sheetName, fileName)
	
xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.sheets(sheetName).Activate
	
' 1)
locate first free
writing:
	
IF
(sheetName = "MANUFACTURING")
THEN
freeRow
FindFreeRowOdd (sheetName,"A12:A1012")
	
ELSE

freeRow = FindFreeRowOdd
(sheetName,"A6:A1006")
	
END IF
IF freeRow = -1
THEN
oops,
no free
rows for pasting.Warn
User.

CloseExcel

Err.Raise 1,,"Production
Schedule:"&fileName&CHR(13)& _
"Sheet "&sheetName&CHR(13)&
 " Sorry,
we can not paste more
than 500 records per sheet in
month."
	
' 2)
thru range of
existing values
testing
if given wo
number is
written
already:
	
existingRow = FindValueRow
(sheetName,"A6:A"&freeRow,mWONumber, "A6")
	
IF
existingRow
-1 THEN

' ok, can safely
paste
data

(sheetName = "SHOP") THEN
PasteShopDataLine
sheetName, freeRow
ELSE

' update
totals table at
head of
manufacturing
page:
IF sheetName = "MANUFACTURING" THEN

PutValue
"MANUFACTURING","N4","=N"&freeRow
ELSE
PutValue "MANUFACTURING","N5","=JOB!N"&freeRow

END IF
PasteDataLine
sheetName,freeRow

END IF
ELSE
oops,
journal
already
contains this
work order.

' ask user
if he
wants
to overwrite the record.
SelectLine sheetName,
existingRow

retValue
MsgBox ("Production
Schedule "&fileName&chr(13)& _
"Sheet "&sheetName&chr(13)&

"Work Order with
number "&mWONumber&" exists
already!"& _
chr(13)&"Do
wish to
replace
it?",4,"Error")
retValue = 6 THEN
replace
(sheetName = "SHOP") THEN

PasteShopDataLine sheetName,
existingRow
ELSE
PasteDataLine
sheetName,existingRow
ELSE

CloseExcel
Err.Raise
1,,"Production Schedule:"&fileName&CHR(13)&
"Sheet "&sheetName&CHR(13)&
"Work
Order
"&mWONumber&"
record insert
canceled at
user request."
	
END IF
END Function
'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Function
PasteOrderDataLine(sheetName,freeRow)
first
copy row for pasting:
PasteLine
"A7:Q7","A"&(freeRow)&":Q"&freeRow,
sheetName
clear
values there
	
ClearValues sheetName,freeRow,1
	
' put wo:
	
PutValue
sheetName,"A"&freeRow,mWONumber
date received:
	
PutValue
sheetName,"B"&freeRow,now
customer name
PutValue sheetName,"C"&freeRow,mBillName
	
' put purch order no
PutValue sheetName,"D"&freeRow,
mPurchOrdrNo
	
' put salesperson
	
PutValue
sheetName,"E"&freeRow, mSalesPerson
descr: cut the first word
MANUFACTURE
present)
	
mWorkDescr
LTrim(mWorkDescr)
cutWord
Left(mWorkDescr,Len("manufacture"))
cutWord
UCase(cutWord)
	
IF
(cutWord = "MANUFACTURE")
THEN
mWorkDescr = Right(mWorkDescr,Len(mWorkDescr)
Len("manufacture"))
	
' shorten the description:
mWorkDescr = Left(mWorkDescr,
MAX_CHARS_DESCR_MO_AND_JO_ORDER)
PutValue sheetName,"F"&freeRow,mWorkDescr
quantity
	
PutValue
sheetName,"G"&freeRow,mNoSignsAlike
credit terms
	
PutValue
sheetName,"H"&freeRow,mCreditTerms
	
' put install ship
via:
	
PutValue
sheetName,"J"&freeRow,mShipVia
	
' put freight pay type
PutValue sheetName,
"K"&freeRow,mPayType
	
' put freight charges
	
PutValue
sheetName,"L"&freeRow,mFreightCharges
sales
volume
	
PutValue
sheetName,"M"&freeRow,mTotalEstCharges
	
' put deposit receive date
PutValue sheetName,"N"&freeRow,mDepositDate
End Function
'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Function
PasteOrderShopDataLine (sheetName, freeRow)
first
copy row for pasting:
PasteLine
"A7:I7","A"&(freeRow)&":I"&freeRow,
sheetName
clear
values there
	
ClearValues sheetName,
freeRow,6
PutValue sheetName,"A"&freeRow,mWONumber
	
' put date
received:
PutValue sheetName,"G"&freeRow,now
	
' put job descr:
first
word MANUFACTURE (if present)
mWorkDescr = LTrim(mWorkDescr)
	
cutWord = Left(mWorkDescr,Len("manufacture"))
	
cutWord = UCase(cutWord)
IF (cutWord
"MANUFACTURE") THEN

mWorkDescr
Right(mWorkDescr,Len(mWorkDescr) - Len("manufacture"))
	
END IF
shorten
description:
mWorkDescr = Left(mWorkDescr,
MAX_CHARS_DESCR_SO_ORDER)
PutValue sheetName,"B"&freeRow,mWorkDescr
labor
code
	
PutValue
sheetName,"I"&freeRow,mLaborExpCode
End Function

Function
PasteShopDataLine
(sheetName,
freeRow)
	
' first copy
pasting:
	
PasteLine "A6:P7","A"&(freeRow-1)&":P"&freeRow, sheetName
	
' now clear values
there

sheetName,freeRow,14

' put date
received:
PutValue sheetName,"B"&freeRow,now
	
' put expense code
PutValue sheetName,"C"&freeRow,mLaborExpCode
	
' put job descr:
first
word MANUFACTURE (if present)
mWorkDescr = LTrim(mWorkDescr)
	
cutWord = Left(mWorkDescr,Len("manufacture"))
	
cutWord = UCase(cutWord)
IF (cutWord
"MANUFACTURE") THEN

mWorkDescr
Right(mWorkDescr,Len(mWorkDescr) - Len("manufacture"))
	
END IF
shorten
description:
	
mWorkDescr
Left(mWorkDescr, MAX_CHARS_DESCR_PROD)
	
PutValue
sheetName,"F"&freeRow,mWorkDescr
	
' put requested completion
date
	
PutValue
sheetName,"J"&freeRow,mCompletionDate
End Function

purch

salesperson

mSalesPerson

IF (cutWord
"MANUFACTURE") THEN

mWorkDescr

Function
	'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	Function ClearValues (sheetName, freeRow,
preserveColumn)
WITH xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.Sheets(sheetName)

cumFormula
=.Cells(freeRow, preserveColumn).Formula
To 16
.Cells(freeRow,
i).Value = ""
Next
.Cells(freeRow,
preserveColumn).Formula
cumFormula
	
END WITH
End Function
'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Function
CloseExcel()
	
IF
(xlsbook.Workbooks.Count >0) THEN

xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.Save
	
END IF
xlsbook.Quit
	End
Function
	'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	Function SelectLine
(sheetName,
WORow)
	
WITH
xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.Sheets(sheetName).Rows(WORow)
.Select

.Cells(WORow,1).Show
WITH
	End
Function 
'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Function
FindFreeRowOdd (sheetName, sheetRange)
result = 0
Each Cell
In xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.Worksheets(sheetName).Range(sheetRange)
(Cell.Row
IsEmpty(Cell.Value)) 
Then

FindFreeRowOdd
Cell.Row

exit
function
Next
	
FindFreeRowOdd
	end
Function
	'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	Function FindFreeRowAny
(sheetName,
sheetRange)
 result
 For Each
Cell In
xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.Worksheets(sheetName).Range(sheetRange)
If (IsEmpty(Cell.Value)) 
Then

FindFreeRowAny
Cell.Row

exit
function
Next
	
FindFreeRowAny
	end
Function
	'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	Function FindValueRow
(sheetName,sheetRange, seekValue,
defCell)
	
dim myCell
WITH xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.Sheets(sheetName)

.Activate
.Range(defCell).Activate
myCell = .Range(sheetRange).Find(seekValue,
xlsbook.ActiveCell,
1, 1,
1, 1,
False)
IF myCell
is Nothing THEN
FindValueRow = -1

ELSE
FindValueRow = myCell.Row

END IF
WITH
	End
function
	'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	Function PasteLine (from,
dest,
sheetName)
	
WITH
xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.Sheets(sheetName)
.Range(from).Copy

.Range(dest).PasteSpecial
WITH 
End Function
'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Function
PutValue(dest, range,
value)
	
xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.sheets(dest).Range(range).Value
 = value
	End

	'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	Function PrintReport
action order:
' 1)
setup
global variables
	
Set fileObj = CreateObject("Scripting.FileSystemObject")

Set xlsbook = CreateObject("Excel.Application")
xlsbook.Visible
True
 xlsbook.StatusBar = "Please be
patient
formatting in
progress..."
2) manipulate
info for production
schedule if
required
	
IF
(mGenProdSchedule
"TRUE")
THEN
check
production schedule
file those name
is constructed from
month
year.
analyze
mCompletionDate- look
month
(IsDate(mCompletionDate))
THEN

fileMonth = Month(CDate(mCompletionDate))

fileYear
Year (CDate(mCompletionDate))

ELSE
CloseExcel

Err.Raise 1,,"Production
Schedule Journal can not be
updated"&CHR(13)&
"because requested completion
date is
invalid!"
EXIT Function

END IF

FileName
prodSchedPath
"\schedule"
fileMonth
fileYear & ".xls"
(fileObj.FileExists(FileName)) THEN

ELSE
create new file:

sourceFile
templatePath 
"\prodSchedule.xls"
fileObj.CopyFile sourceFile, FileName, FALSE

' now can open
file,
setup

xlsbook.Workbooks.Open
FileName
(xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.ReadOnly = TRUE) then

xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.Close
TRUE

ErrorText
"Production
Schedule Journal " + FileName
"+chr(13)

ErrorText = ErrorText +"be
updated
because
it is
used by
another
user now."
ErrorText
ErrorText
chr(13)+"Do
wish to
retry
to open
Production Schedule
Journal?"

msgRetVal = MsgBox(ErrorText,5+16,"Error")
(msgRetVal = 4)
then

' retry 
UserAction = FALSE
else

CloseExcel
Err.Raise
1,,"Production Schedule
Journal
"&fileName&" was not updated because it
is locked!"
exit Function

end if
else
UserAction = TRUE
Loop While UserAction
FALSE

' set A1
cell in
three
tabs to
current
month-year of
file name

PutValue
"MANUFACTURING","A1",
fileMonth&"/"&fileYear
PutValue "JOB","A1", fileMonth&"/"&fileYear

PutValue
"SHOP","A1", fileMonth&"/"&fileYear

' work
with sheet depending on
work order type:
if (mWorkOrderType = "MO-")
then

UpdateProdSheet "MANUFACTURING",
fileName
if (mWorkOrderType = "JO-")
then

UpdateProdSheet "JOB",
fileName
if (mWorkOrderType = "SO-")
then

UpdateProdSheet "SHOP", fileName

end if
(mWorkOrderType
then

CloseExcel
Err.Raise
1,,"Production Schedule
Journal
updated
because
Work Order type
selected!"

exit
Function
xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.save
' 3)
manipulate info
order
journal
if required
if (mGenOrderJournal = "TRUE") then

fileMonth = Month(CDate(mCreateDate))
fileYear = Year
(CDate(mCreateDate))
FileName = orderJournPath
"\orders"
fileMonth
fileYear & ".xls"
(fileObj.FileExists(FileName)) then

else
create new file:

sourceFile
templatePath 
"\OrderJournal.xls"
fileObj.CopyFile sourceFile, FileName, FALSE

' now can open
file,
setup

xlsbook.Workbooks.Open
FileName
(xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.ReadOnly = TRUE) then

xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.Close
TRUE

ErrorText
"Order Journal " + FileName
"+chr(13)

ErrorText = ErrorText +"be
updated
because
it is
used by
another
user now."
ErrorText
ErrorText
chr(13)+"Do
wish to
retry
to open
Order
Journal?"

msgRetVal = MsgBox(ErrorText,5+16,"Error")
(msgRetVal = 4)
then

' retry 
UserAction = FALSE
else

CloseExcel
Err.Raise
1,,"Order
Entry
Journal
"&fileName&" was not updated because it
is locked!"
exit Function

end if
else
UserAction = TRUE
Loop While UserAction
FALSE

' set A1
cell in
three
tabs to
current
month-year of
file name

PutValue
"MANUFACTURING","A1",
fileMonth&"/"&fileYear
PutValue "JOB","A1", fileMonth&"/"&fileYear

PutValue
"SHOP","A1", fileMonth&"/"&fileYear

' work
with sheet depending on
work order type:
if (mWorkOrderType = "MO-")
then

UpdateOrderSheet
"MANUFACTURING", fileName

end if
(mWorkOrderType
"JO-") then
UpdateOrderSheet "JOB",
fileName
if (mWorkOrderType = "SO-")
then

UpdateOrderSheet
"SHOP",
fileName
if (mWorkOrderType = "") then
CloseExcel

Err.Raise 1,,"Can not update
Order
Entry
Journal
because
Work Order type
selected."
xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.save
	
xlsbook.StatusBar = FALSE
4) ask user
if he
wishes to
hide excel again.
if yes-
kill excel.
msgRetVal
MsgBox("Do you wish
to close Excel now?",4+32,"Question")
if (msgRetVal
6) then
response Yes.

xlsbook.Quit
else
	
end if
End Function

Function
HandleDates
' action
order:
1) setup global
variables
fileObj
CreateObject("Scripting.FileSystemObject")
xlsbook
CreateObject("Excel.Application")

xlsbook.Visible = True
xlsbook.StatusBar
"Please
be patient - formatting
in progress..."
' 2)
manipulate info
production schedule
if required
IF (mGenProdSchedule = "TRUE") THEN

' check for production
schedule file
those
name is
constructed
from month and year.
'a ) analyze mCompletionDate-
look for month
IF (IsDate(mCompletionDate)) THEN
fileMonth
Month(CDate(mCompletionDate))
fileYear = Year
(CDate(mCompletionDate))
ELSE

CloseExcel
Err.Raise
1,,"Production Schedule
Journal
be updated"&CHR(13)& _

"because
specified
completion date
is invalid!"

EXIT
Function
FileName = prodSchedPath & "\schedule" & fileMonth & "_" & fileYear
".xls"
IF not (fileObj.FileExists(FileName))
THEN

CloseExcel
raise
an error about missing file
then quit
Err.Raise
1,,"Production Schedule
Journal
updated
because
schedule file
"&FileName&" was not found!"

Exit Function

END IF
open the file, and setup it
xlsbook.Workbooks.Open FileName
if (xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.ReadOnly
TRUE)
then
xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.Close TRUE

ErrorText = "Production Schedule
Journal
FileName + " can not "+chr(13)

ErrorText
ErrorText
+"be updated because it
is used
by another user
now."

ErrorText = ErrorText + chr(13)+"Do you wish
to retry to
open Production
Schedule Journal?"
msgRetVal
MsgBox(ErrorText,5+16,"Error")
if (msgRetVal
4) then
retry

UserAction
FALSE

else
CloseExcel

Err.Raise 1,,"Production
Schedule Journal "&fileName&"
updated
because
it is
locked!"

exit
Function

else

UserAction
TRUE

end if

Loop
While
UserAction = FALSE

to current month-year
of file

'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Function
CloseExcel()
	
IF
(xlsbook.application.Workbooks.Count >=
1) THEN

xlsbook.activeWorkbook.Save
	
END IF
xlsBook.application.Quit
	End
Function
	'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	Function FindValueRow
(sheetName,sheetRange, seekColumn,seekValue)
result = 0
Each Cell
In xlsbook.activeWorkbook.Worksheets(sheetName).Range(sheetRange)
Cell.Value = seekValue Then
result = 0 Then
 result
Cell.Row
Next
If result
<> 0 Then
 MsgBox
("For
debug
only:I found it!")
 FindValueRow
result
Else
MsgBox ("For debug only: Sorry,
no solutions found!")
FindValueRow = -1
 End If
End function
'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Function
PutValue(dest, range,
value)
	
xlsbook.application.activeworkbook.sheets(dest).Range(range).Value
 = value
	End
Function
	'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
	Function UpdateOrderSheet
(sheetName)
xlsbook.application.activeworkbook.sheets(sheetName).Activate
search for line
with the same
WORow
FindValueRow (sheetName,"a1:a180",1,mWONumber)
	
if
WORow
-1 then

' sorry,
requested
order
found. Warn
User about error.

ErrorText = "Sorry, but requested "&sheetName&" order with
number "&mWONumber&" was not found!"
ErrorText
ErrorText
chr(10)+"Can not update
work order date
of completion."

CloseExcel

Err.Raise 1,,ErrorText
else
create new date
of completion;
if (sheetName
"SHOP")
then

PutValue
sheetName, "H"&WORow,

else
PutValue sheetName,
"I"&WORow, now
	
end if
end Function
'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Function
UpdateProdSheet
(sheetName)
xlsbook.application.activeworkbook.sheets(sheetName).Activate
search for line
with the same
WORow
FindValueRow (sheetName,"a1:a180",1,mWONumber)
	
if
WORow
-1 then

' sorry,
requested
order
found. Warn
User about error.

ErrorText = "Sorry, but requested "&sheetName&" order with
number "&mWONumber&" was not found!"
ErrorText
ErrorText
chr(10)+"Can not update
work order date
of completion."

CloseExcel

Err.Raise 1,,ErrorText
else
	
'---------------------------------------------------------------------
Feature
implemented
yet. Waiting for request from
Brian.
	
CloseExcel
Err.Raise
"Updating
Production Schedule: feature not implemented yet.Please
implement."

' create
date of
completion;
if (sheetName
"SHOP")
then
PutValue sheetName,
"H"&WORow, date(now)

else

PutValue
sheetName, "I"&WORow,
date(now)
	
end if
end Function
'-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Function
PrintReport
' action
order:
1) setup global
variables
fileObj
CreateObject("Scripting.FileSystemObject")
xlsbook
CreateObject("Excel.Application")

xlsbook.application.Visible = True
' 2)
manipulate info
production schedule
if required
if (mGenProdSchedule = "TRUE") then

' check for production
schedule file
those
name is
constructed
this way:
analyze
mCompletionDate- look
month
(IsDate(mCompletionDate))
then

fileMonth = Month(CDate(mCompletionDate))

fileYear
Year (CDate(mCompletionDate))

else
fileMonth
Month
(now)
fileYear = Year(now)
FileName = prodSchedPath & "\schedule" & fileMonth & "_" & fileYear
".xls"
if (fileObj.FileExists(FileName))
then
else

CloseExcel
raise
an error about missing file
then quit
Err.Raise
1,,"Production Schedule
Journal
updated
because
schedule file
"&FileName&" was not found!"

Exit Function

end if
open the file, and setup it
xlsbook.application.Workbooks.Open FileName
if (xlsbook.application.activeworkbook.ReadOnly
TRUE)
then
xlsbook.application.activeworkbook.Close TRUE

ErrorText = "Production Schedule
Journal
FileName + " can not "+chr(13)

ErrorText
ErrorText
+"be updated because it
is used
by another user
now."

ErrorText = ErrorText + chr(13)+"Do you wish
to retry to
open Production
Schedule Journal?"
msgRetVal
MsgBox(ErrorText,5+16,"Error")
if (msgRetVal
4) then
retry

UserAction
FALSE

else
CloseExcel

Err.Raise 1,,"Production
Schedule Journal was not updated because it
is locked!"
exit Function

end if
else
UserAction = TRUE
Loop While UserAction
FALSE

' work
with sheet depending on
work order type:
if (mWorkOrderType = "MO-")
then

UpdateProdSheet "MANUFACTURING"
if (mWorkOrderType = "JO-")
then

UpdateProdSheet "JOB"
if (mWorkOrderType = "SO-")
then

UpdateProdSheet "SHOP"

end if
(mWorkOrderType
then

MsgBox
"Can not update
Production Schedule
Journal
because
Work Order type
selected.",0,"Error"
xlsbook.application.activeworkbook.save
' 3)
manipulate info
order
journal
if required
if (mGenOrderJournal = "TRUE") then

' check for production
schedule file
those
name is
constructed
this way:
analyze
mCompletionDate- look
month
(IsDate(mCompletionDate))
then

fileMonth = Month(CDate(mCompletionDate))

fileYear
Year (CDate(mCompletionDate))

else
fileMonth
Month
(now)
fileYear = Year(now)
FileName = orderJournPath
"\orders"
fileMonth
fileYear & ".xls"
(fileObj.FileExists(FileName)) then

else
CloseExcel

' raise an
error
about
missing
file then
quit

Err.Raise 1,,"Order Journal was not updated because orders
file "&FileName&"
found!"

Exit
Function

' now can open
file,
setup

xlsbook.application.Workbooks.Open
FileName
if (xlsbook.application.activeworkbook.ReadOnly
TRUE)
then
xlsbook.application.activeworkbook.Close TRUE

ErrorText = "Order
Journal
FileName + " can not "+chr(13)

ErrorText
ErrorText
+"be updated because it
is used
by another user
now."

ErrorText = ErrorText + chr(13)+"Do you wish
to retry to
open Order Journal?"
msgRetVal
MsgBox(ErrorText,5+16,"Error")
if (msgRetVal
4) then
retry

UserAction
FALSE

else
CloseExcel

Err.Raise 1,,"Order Entry Journal was not updated because it
is locked!"
exit Function

end if
else
UserAction = TRUE
Loop While UserAction
FALSE

' work
with sheet depending on
work order type:
if (mWorkOrderType = "MO-")
then

UpdateOrderSheet
"MANUFACTURING"

end if
(mWorkOrderType
"JO-") then
UpdateOrderSheet "JOB"
if (mWorkOrderType = "SO-")
then

UpdateOrderSheet
"SHOP"
if (mWorkOrderType = "") then
CloseExcel

Err.Raise 1,,"Can not update
Order
Entry
Journal
because
Work Order type
selected."
xlsbook.application.activeworkbook.save
' 4)
user if
he wishes
to hide
excel
again. if
yes- kill
excel.
	
msgRetVal = MsgBox("Do
wish to
close
Excel
now?",4+32,"Question")
	
if
(msgRetVal = 6)
then ' response

xlsbook.application.quit
	
else
	End

Function OpenFile
(path, FileName)
	
set fileObj = CreateObject("Scripting.FileSystemObject")

Set xlsbook = CreateObject("Excel.Application")
xlsbook.Visible
True
	
fullName
FileName
	
IF
(fileObj.FileExists(fullName)) THEN
xlsBook.Quit

' raise an
error
about
missing
file then
quit

Err.Raise 1,,"Requested to
open file
"&fullName&" was not found!"

Exit Function

END IF
open the file
xlsbook.Workbooks.Open fullName
End Function

xlsbook
dim ColWidth
ColWidth
Array
(0 ,11.5,11,12,
9, 20, 20,10)
Function
PrintReport
xlsbook
CreateObject("Excel.Application")
xlsbook.application.Visible
True
 xlsbook.application.Workbooks.Add CsvFileName
 WITH
xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.ActiveSheet
.Cells.Font.Name = "Arial
Narrow"

xlsbook.StatusBar = "Please be
patient
formatting in
progress..."
to 7
.Columns(i).ColumnWidth
ColWidth(i-1)

.Columns(i).Borders.LineStyle = 1

NEXT
hide column
.Columns(1).Hidden = TRUE

' insert
rows for header;
.Rows(1).Insert

.Rows(1).Insert
.Rows(1).Insert

.Range("A1:A3").Value = "EMPTY"
.Range("B1").Value = "Job
Number:"
.Range("B2").Value = "Applied
Filter:"
.Range("B1").HorizontalAlignment = -4152 'xlHAlignRight

.Range("B2").HorizontalAlignment
-4152
'xlHAlignRight
.Range("C1").Value = jobNumber
.Range("C2").Value = filterText

' locate
last entered row
lastRow
.Columns(1).End(4).Row
start
iterating
thru range:
.Range("A1:Z"&lastRow).Font.Name = "Arial
Narrow"

.Range("A1:Z"&lastRow).Font.Size
Each Cell
In .Range("A4:A"&lastRow)
rowNo
Cell.Row

SELECT
CASE Cell.Value
Case "EMPTY"
do nothing

Case
"HDR1"
this is
section
department declaration.
.Rows(rowNo).Font.Bold = TRUE

.Rows(rowNo).Font.Size
.Range("A"&rowNo&":H"&rowNo).Borders(4).LineStyle
double underline

Case
"HDR2"
format header:
.Rows(rowNo).Font.Bold = TRUE

.Rows(rowNo).Font.Size

.Rows(rowNo).WrapText = TRUE
.Rows(rowNo).VerticalAlignment = -4160 ' xlVAlignTop 

.Rows(rowNo).HorizontalAlignment
-4108
xlHAlignCenter


.Range("A"&rowNo&":H"&rowNo).Borders(4).LineStyle = 9 ' double
underline
Case "ROW"

' tell
first
column to
be size
of 9:
.Range("B"&rowNo&":B"&rowNo).Font.Size = 9

Case
"GPDDTL"
remove the first symbol- this
is necessary to
force
excel
display
numbers
as text

.Range("B"&rowNo&":B"&rowNo).Value
(.Range("B"&rowNo&":B"&rowNo).Value,2)
Case Else
do nothing -skip line

END SELECT

Next
setup
page headers:
insert report
title
page #s
.PageSetup.RightHeader = "&RDate of
Report:
.PageSetup.CenterHeader
="&CLABOR
RECORDS
PRINTOUT"

.PageSetup.CenterFooter = "&CPage &P
of &N"
	
.PageSetup.Orientation
.PageSetup.CenterHorizontally
FALSE
 .PageSetup.CenterVertically = FALSE
	
.PageSetup.LeftMargin = xlsbook.Application.InchesToPoints(0.5)
.PageSetup.RightMargin = xlsbook.Application.InchesToPoints(0.25)
 .PageSetup.TopMargin
xlsbook.Application.InchesToPoints(0.77)
.PageSetup.BottomMargin
xlsbook.Application.InchesToPoints(0.75)
.PageSetup.HeaderMargin
xlsbook.Application.InchesToPoints(0.5)
 .PageSetup.FooterMargin = xlsbook.Application.InchesToPoints(0.5)
.PageSetup.PrintHeadings = FALSE
.PageSetup.PrintGridlines
FALSE

' remove
column A:

.Columns(1).Delete

' make
cell A1
active:
.Range("A1").Activate
xlsbook.StatusBar
FALSE
WITH
save current sheet in
case user
won't
be asked various questions:
 xlsbook.activeworkbook.Saved
TRUE
xlsbook.activeworkbook.activesheet.Range("A1").Activate
	End
Function

dim ColWidth
ColWidth
Array
(0 ,11.5,20,26,
9, 9,
	Function PrintReport
 Set xlsbook = CreateObject("Excel.Application")
 xlsbook.application.Visible = True
xlsbook.application.Workbooks.Add
CsvFileName
WITH xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.ActiveSheet

.Cells.Font.Name
"Arial Narrow"
xlsbook.StatusBar
"Please
be patient - formatting
in progress..."

FOR i = 1 to

.Columns(i).ColumnWidth = ColWidth(i-1) 
.Columns(i).Borders.LineStyle
NEXT


' hide
column A:

.Columns(1).Hidden
TRUE
insert 3 rows
header;

.Rows(1).Insert
.Rows(1).Insert

.Rows(1).Insert
.Range("A1:A3").Value
"EMPTY"

.Range("B1").Value
"Job Number:"

.Range("B2").Value
"Applied Filter:"

.Range("B1").HorizontalAlignment
-4152
'xlHAlignRight
.Range("B2").HorizontalAlignment = -4152 'xlHAlignRight

jobNumber = Replace (jobNumber,Chr(34)+Chr(34),Chr(34))
.Range("C1").Value = jobNumber
filterText = Replace (filterText,Chr(34)+Chr(34),Chr(34))

.Range("C2").Value
filterText
locate last
entered

lastRow = .Columns(1).End(4).Row

' start iterating thru
range: 

.Range("A1:Z"&lastRow).Font.Name
"Arial Narrow"
.Range("A1:Z"&lastRow).Font.Size = 10

For Each
Cell In
.Range("A4:A"&lastRow)

rowNo = Cell.Row
SELECT CASE
Cell.Value

Case
"EMPTY"

' do
nothing
Case "HDR1"

' this
is section and department
declaration. 

.Rows(rowNo).Font.Bold
TRUE
.Rows(rowNo).Font.Size = 10

.Range("A"&rowNo&":G"&rowNo).Borders(4).LineStyle = 9 ' double
underline
Case "HDR2"

' format
header:

.Rows(rowNo).Font.Bold
TRUE
.Rows(rowNo).Font.Size = 10
.Rows(rowNo).WrapText
TRUE

.Rows(rowNo).VerticalAlignment
-4160
xlVAlignTop
.Rows(rowNo).HorizontalAlignment = -4108 ' xlHAlignCenter
.Range("A"&rowNo&":G"&rowNo).Borders(4).LineStyle
double underline


Case
"ROW"
tell the first column
to be
size of

.Range("B"&rowNo&":G"&rowNo).Font.Size

' the C column
should be
left aligned:
.Range("C"&rowNo).HorizontalAlignment
-4131
'xlHAlignLeft
tell the C column
that it
is Text
.Range("C"&rowNo).NumberFormat = "@"

' the C column
unnecessary
symbol at
start-must remove
.Range("C"&rowNo).Value
(.Range("C"&rowNo).Value ,2)
Case Else
do nothing -skip line

END SELECT

Next
setup
page headers:
insert report
title
page #s
.PageSetup.RightHeader = "&RDate of
Report:
.PageSetup.CenterHeader
="&CMATERIAL RECORDS PRINTOUT"
.PageSetup.CenterFooter
"&CPage
&P of
.PageSetup.Orientation = 1
	
.PageSetup.CenterHorizontally = FALSE
.PageSetup.CenterVertically
FALSE
.PageSetup.LeftMargin
xlsbook.Application.InchesToPoints(0.5)
 .PageSetup.RightMargin
xlsbook.Application.InchesToPoints(0.25)
.PageSetup.TopMargin = xlsbook.Application.InchesToPoints(0.77)
 .PageSetup.BottomMargin = xlsbook.Application.InchesToPoints(0.75)
 .PageSetup.HeaderMargin = xlsbook.Application.InchesToPoints(0.5)
.PageSetup.FooterMargin
xlsbook.Application.InchesToPoints(0.5)
 .PageSetup.PrintHeadings
FALSE
 .PageSetup.PrintGridlines = FALSE
remove column
.Columns(1).Delete
make cell
A1 active:
	
.Range("A1").Activate
 xlsbook.StatusBar = FALSE
 END WITH
 ' save
current
sheet
in case
user won't be
asked
various
questions:
xlsbook.activeworkbook.Saved = TRUE
 xlsbook.activeworkbook.activesheet.Range("A1").Activate
End Function

xlsbook
dim ColWidth
ColWidth
Array
(0 ,10,
Function
PrintReport
(fileName)
 Set xlsbook = CreateObject("Excel.Application")
 xlsbook.application.Visible = True
xlsbook.application.Workbooks.Add
fileName
 WITH
xlsbook.ActiveWorkbook.ActiveSheet
xlsbook.StatusBar
"Please
be patient - formatting
in progress..."

FOR i = 1 to

.Columns(i).ColumnWidth = ColWidth(i-1) 

.Columns(i).Borders.LineStyle = 1

NEXT
hide column
.Columns(1).Hidden = TRUE

' insert
rows for empty header;
.Rows(1).Insert

.Range("A1").Value
"EMPTY"

' locate
last entered row
lastRow
.Columns(1).End(4).Row
start
iterating
thru range:
.Range("A1:Z"&lastRow).Font.Name = "Arial
Narrow"

.Range("A1:Z"&lastRow).Font.Size
Each Cell
In .Range("A1:A"&lastRow)
rowNo
Cell.Row

SELECT
CASE Cell.Value
Case "EMPTY"
do nothing
.Rows(Cell.Row).Borders.LineStyle
Case "SORT"

.Rows(Cell.Row).Borders.LineStyle = 0

Case
"HDR"

' format
current
as header

.Rows(rowNo).Font.Bold
TRUE
.Rows(rowNo).Font.Size = 10

.Range("A"&rowNo&":E"&rowNo).Borders(4).LineStyle = 9 ' double
underline

.Rows(rowNo).WrapText = FALSE
.Rows(rowNo).VerticalAlignment = -4160 'xlVAlignTop
Case "ROW"
make alignment,
etc:

.Range("B"&rowNo).HorizontalAlignment = -4131 'xlHAlignLeft
Case Else
do nothing -skip line

END SELECT

Next
setup
page headers:
insert report
title
page #s
.PageSetup.RightHeader = "&RDate of
Report:
.PageSetup.CenterHeader
="&CUNPOSTED INVOICES
REPORT"

.PageSetup.CenterFooter = "&CPage &P
of &N"
	
.PageSetup.Orientation
.PageSetup.CenterHorizontally
TRUE
.PageSetup.CenterVertically
FALSE
.PageSetup.LeftMargin
xlsbook.Application.InchesToPoints(0.5)
 .PageSetup.RightMargin
xlsbook.Application.InchesToPoints(0.25)
.PageSetup.TopMargin = xlsbook.Application.InchesToPoints(0.77)
 .PageSetup.BottomMargin = xlsbook.Application.InchesToPoints(0.75)
 .PageSetup.HeaderMargin = xlsbook.Application.InchesToPoints(0.5)
.PageSetup.FooterMargin
xlsbook.Application.InchesToPoints(0.5)
 .PageSetup.PrintHeadings
FALSE
 .PageSetup.PrintGridlines = FALSE
remove column
.Columns(1).Delete
 xlsbook.StatusBar = FALSE
 END WITH
 ' save
current
sheet
in case
user won't be
asked
